                    (function() {
                        if(window.innerWidth >= 1550){
                            $('#leftStaticSlot').removeClass('hidden');
                            var repositionStaticVertical2 = () => {
                                let elmntWidth = 1220;
                                let windowWidth = window.innerWidth;
                                let horizontal = (windowWidth-elmntWidth)/2-170;
                                $('#leftStaticSlot').css('left', horizontal);
                            }
                            $(window).resize(repositionStaticVertical2);
                            repositionStaticVertical2();
                        
                            if(window['nitroAds']){
                                window['nitroAds'].createAd("leftStaticSlot", {"floor": 0.2, "refreshLimit": 10, "refreshTime": 30, "sizes": [[160,600]], "report":{"enabled":true,"wording":"Report Ad","position":"bottom-right"}});
                            } 
                        } 
                    })();

    var toggleRegionFilter = function (display) {
